<review>I hate service in 626. They barely understand you. And they're RUDE. I called the arcade adjacent to it and they said it was already closed at 9pm. We went there anyways and it was still open... and stayed open until 1am!

Note: ARCADE OPENS UNTIL 1AM (for sat at least).

I did win a cute milk carton guy hehe. Tip: Try to grab the one with the most surface area exposed to the claw.

<Date>1434097887936< /Date><gmap_id>0x80c32a618a951f57:0xa7828aa41fd424ee<//gmap_id>< text>
I ordered a passionfruit green tea with crystal boba. Their crystal boba is basically clear boba which is pretty unique. I tend to switch up my order here because I haven't exactly found my perfect drink from here yet. I have tried the watermelon green tea as well and it's good. My only complaint with that is that the drink separates the juice and the foam so when you get towards the bottom, all you get is watermelon foam. The passionfruit green tea is pretty good, better than a lot of other places. Their food is also very good. The fish cakes and popcorn chicken are very tasty. The fish cakes are kind of like a mochi texture and is topped with a really good seasoning.

Tea Bar's popcorn chicken is the best, it's really crispy on the outside and full of flavor on the inside. It's better than any other place where I've tried popcorn chicken. The atmosphere is very alright. Near the cash register, there are a lot of jungle decorations with animals on the wall. However, this theme doesn't carry onto the rest of the sitting area.

That area is very plain but I enjoy sitting there. It's good for just hanging out with friends and talking. The restroom is shared with a few other stores in the same area.

It requires a key but Tea Bar's got stolen so you have to ask one of the other stores. Overall, I do enjoy coming here and would definitely come back.< /text>

<rate>1< /rate>< Text>
My family and I recently had a very negative experience with Dentist Sosa. Our 4 year old damaged a tooth about a year ago that required repair. Upon arriving at the office I was informed that I would not be allowed back with my daughter for the procedure and she permitted my wife to go begrudgingly due to her age. I was put off by this but let it slide as we have been seeing this person for about 8 years at the time. Now, that repaired tooth needs to be redone and we were told under no uncertain terms that we were not welcome to be present during the procedure. In addition to being very coarse she offered no reasoning as to why and then very passive aggressively printed up a form with her office policies and handed it to my wife and I.
Though we were put off, very upset and despite our better judgment we acquiesced as we were afraid of causing our daughter undo pain by delaying the procedure. At that point Dr. Sosa said she wasn't willing to do the procedure at that time because my Wife was visibly upset. At that point we left and will never go back. Her lack of bedside manner, lack of respect for our time and disregard for our daughter (Who wasn't about to go back without her mother at the very least) has severed a 9 year relationship.
I am of the opinion that a Pediatric dentist is a specialty that exists to cater to Children and their parents. If you don't do that you are simply a regular dentist. My 4 year old can't advocate for herself and she is scared by the very prospect of going to the dentist for a simple cleaning, much less something that is as scary to her as a broken tooth. Since Dentist Sosa took away any Utility she can actually provide as a "Pediatric" Dentist,  We will simply take our Daughter to our Family dentist or find a Pediatric Dentist that actually has our children's feelings and best interests in mind. After very little research it doesn't look like it will be hard.< /Text>

<user>115904139467410709292<//user>< review>
Today we saw Dr. Rossanne Sosa located at 10715 Tierrasanta Boulevard. The visit began well with the dentist coming out to say hello to my son and beginning with a discussion about good dental care. She then examined my son's teeth and applied a fluoride varnish.

As we were discussing treatment things began going downhill. She told me I would have to wean my son from breastfeeding. When I replied that I would not do so she became defensive. She repeated information about how a cavity is formed and told me breastfeeding was the problem. I said that food causes cavities and breastmilk is food but I wasn't going to stop feeding my son. I also told her I had done some research regarding breastmilk and cavities and knew that breastmilk contains cavity fighting ingredients. She replied that if I had done research I obviously wasn't going to listen to anything she had to say. I then asked her what training she had in regards to how breastmilk affects baby teeth and she told me we were done and walked out.

Overall I felt like she didn't have respect for me as a parent. She is obviously the expert on teeth and as such should inform me about the state of my son's teeth and her suggestions on what to do about it. But as the parent I get to take in all that information and decide what to do! And she definitely didn't respect that. She didn't like that I questioned her or that I did research.

It was truly a disappointing visit.<//review>

< Text>
My family and I recently had a very negative experience with Dentist Sosa. Our 4 year old damaged a tooth about a year ago that required repair. She repeated information about how a cavity is formed and told me breastfeeding was the problem. I said that food causes cavities and breastmilk is food but I wasn't going to stop feeding my son. I also told her I had done some research regarding breastmilk and cavities and knew that breastmilk contains cavity fighting ingredients. She replied that if I had done research I obviously wasn't going to listen to anything she had to say. Overall I felt like she didn't have respect for me as a parent. < Review>
Today we saw Dr. Rossanne Sosa located at 10715 Tierrasanta Boulevard. The visit began well with the dentist coming out to say hello to my son and beginning with a discussion about good dental care. She then examined my son's teeth and applied a fluoride varnish.

As we were discussing treatment things began going downhill. She told me I would have to wean my son from breastfeeding. When I replied that I would not do so she became defensive. She repeated information about how a cavity is formed and told me breastfeeding was the problem. I said that food causes cavities and breastmilk is food but I wasn't going to stop feeding my son. I also told her I had done some research regarding breastmilk and cavities and knew that breastmilk contains cavity fighting ingredients. She replied that if I had done research I obviously wasn't going to listen to anything she had to say. I then asked her what training she had in regards to how breastmilk affects baby teeth and she told me we were done and walked out.

Overall I felt like she didn't have respect for me as a parent. She is obviously the expert on teeth and as such should inform me about the state of my son's teeth and her suggestions on what to do about it. But as the parent I get to take in all that information and decide what to do! And she definitely didn't respect that. She didn't like that I questioned her or that I did research.

It was truly a disappointing visit.<//Review>

<rating>5</rating>< Review>
An honest review means a lot to me and I think it helps any business or organization to achieve it ultimate goal. Also from the customer perspective, a review helps others to understand what they are likely to expect. Here is my review for Ocean Nissan based on my recent business with them

Sales Department
----------------

1. No one was pushy (A typical sales style that possibly most hate).

2. Right from the moment you park your car and step in, people are happy to see you and willing  to help you. Always expect a big smile from most of them.

3. Hooman Keyvan is an amazing person and man who sticks to his words.. Always a winner for me in any profession. If you want your next Nissan talk to him. A genuine person.

4. The Sales Management team is very good and would tell you what they can and what they cannot do.

Service Department
------------------

1. The service department was responsible for applying the Enviroguard and they took some time as a loaner was available.

2. They service quality was good and I am hoping to get outstanding service as I step in to get my servicing in the future done.

3. I wish they have more loaner, so that customers donot need to wait for longer to get their work done.

Dealership
-------------

1. Clean and nice ambiance.

2. I heard that the owners visit it regularly and that I am sure shows their passion in the business.

3. Good selection of vehicles to choose from.

4. Car Doc and Enviroguard are good options that not many dealerships provide.

5. They want new and existing customers to come to them and that tell me that they take pride in their service and customer.

6. Personally would have loved to see some more tea options in the waiting area.:)

Hope what I have written helps others and hope the dealership and its people exceed my expectations all the time.< /Review>
